Single gap:
FKTK - AZIDA BINTI AZMI

FKTK - SITI SARAH BINTI IBRAHIM
Border gap:
FKTE - ADILAH BINTI HASHIM
FKTE - MAIZATUL NURUL BARIAH AHMAD

FKTE - NURHAFIZA BINTI AZIZAN

FKC - WAN NURUL AIFFAH ISMAIL

FKTE - EN MOHD HAFIZ BIN ARSHAD
FPK - ZUHAIRAH IDRUS
Must stay longer:
FKTE - AHMAD MUHYIDDIN BIN YUSOF
FKTE - DIYYA HIDAYAH BINTI ABD RAHMAN

FKC - SAFWATI IBRAHIM
